## Text Elements
#saal ^4kQG4nJZ

shortest path w. negative weights ^of1GKMzF

assume no negative cycles ^r8I0InPa

E path w. at most n-1 edges ^ICm5DGP9

OPT(i,v) ^PekWon1c

shortest length from v to t, w. < i edges  ^P1IzXoX2

OPT(n-1,s) ^gg1ImGQY

optimal length from s⟶t ^HOKB4oS5

OPT(0,t)=0 ^EqJP2Cvf

(v≇t) OPT(0,v)=ꝏ ^zrZDeHEE

find w, that added to opt. path is minimum ^zCJah4wa

bellman-ford algorithm ^dOWaftL3

initialize M[0,...,n-1][v e V(G)]
M[0][t]=0
M[0][v]=ꝏ (v≇t)
for i=1,...,n-1:
    for v e V(G):
        M[i,v]=M[i-1,v]
        for w s.t. (v,w) e E:
            φ=Cv,w + M[i-1][w]
            if φ<M[i,v]:
                M[i,v]=φ

P=[t]
i=n-1
while P[0]≇v:
    v=P[0]
    if M[i][v]≇M[i-1][v]:
        Let w s.t. M[i,v]=Cv,w + M[i-1][w]
        P=[w]+P
    i-=1
return P ^30XnMv6W

running 1 more step if cost decreases ∴ E negative cycle ^6Xnyj40Z

subset-sum ^00Rl2Xt4
